class="page-wrapper" data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.9.1.0.3.$recap"><div class="ad-pencil" data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.9.1.0.3.$recap.0"><div class="ad-wrapper" data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.9.1.0.3.$recap.0.0" id="matchcenter-pencil-middle1"></div></div><div class="clearfix recap" data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.9.1.0.3.$recap.1"><div class="article-container block" data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0"><div class="article-content-wrapper" data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0"><h1 class="article-title" data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.0">Canada 1, Honduras 0 | CONCACAF World Cup Qualifying Match Recap</h1><div class="byline" data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.1"><address class="author" data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.1.0"><a data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.1.0.0" href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/author/Daniel Squizzato" rel="author">Daniel Squizzato</a></address><time class="pubdate" data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.1.1" datetime="2015-11-14">Nov 14, 2015</time></div><div data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.2"></div><div class="gigya-share" data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.4" id="article-share"></div><img class="article-primary-image" data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.5" src="http://league-mp7static.mlsdigital.net/styles/image_default/s3/images/OuimetteCanHon.jpg"><article class="article" data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.6"><p>VANCOUVER, B.C. --\xc2\xa0They don\xe2\x80\x99t ask how, they just ask how many\xe2\x80\x94and that adage has perhaps never been more meaningful\xc2\xa0than it was for Canada on Friday night.</p>\n<p>A bizarre, deflected goal was enough for the Canadians to open the semifinal round of World Cup qualifying with a 1-0 win in front of 20,108 fans at BC Place in Vancouver. <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/will-johnson">Will Johnson</a> got credit, though the last touch appeared to come off the backside of <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/cyle-larin">Cyle Larin</a>, laying on the ground in the Honduran goal area.</p>\n<p>With Mexico\xe2\x80\x99s 3-0 win over El Salvador, Canada sit\xc2\xa0second in Group A, ahead of their match in San Salvador on Tuesday. Honduras head\xc2\xa0back home to face <em>El Tri</em> that same day.</p>\n<ul>\n<li><strong><a href="http://matchcenter.mlssoccer.com/matchcenter/2015-11-13-canada-mens-national-team-vs-honduras/stats">CHECK OUT TEAM STATISTICS FROM THE GAME</a></strong></li>\n</ul>\n<p>In front of a raucous crowd led by a boisterous contingent of the Voyageurs, Canada controlled the possession in the early going. That led to the first decent chance of the game in the 11th\xc2\xa0minute, when Junior Hoilett and Atiba Hutchinson worked a one-two down the left wing, and Hoilett won a dangerous free kick. But <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/marcel-de-jong">Marcel de Jong</a> lofted the set piece into the waiting arms of Honduran keeper Noel Valladares.</p>\n<p>The Canadians tested their luck\xc2\xa0somewhat in the first half, hitting\xc2\xa0plenty of backpasses\xe2\x80\x94and they nearly got burned in the 27th\xc2\xa0minute, when Carlos Discua capitalized on an Adam Straith turnover and cracked a shot just high of Milan Borjan\xe2\x80\x99s goal.</p>\n<p>Canada hit back four minutes later; an excellent cross-field pass from Hutchinson found Julian de Guzman unmarked 30 yards in front of goal. Valladares stretched to make an excellent save, parrying the Ottawa Fury midfielder\xe2\x80\x99s shot over the bar.</p>\n<p>In the 38th\xc2\xa0minute, Canada had their\xc2\xa0breakthrough. Hoilett did more good work on the left wing, sending in an excellent cross that found the head of Johnson, then the back of a prone Larin and, eventually, the back of the Honduran goal.</p>\n<p>Honduras had the first opportunity of the second half, with Erick Andino getting sight of Borjan\xe2\x80\x99s goal from 20 yards out within the first minute. But the midfielder lifted his shot harmlessly over the crossbar.</p>\n<p>Canada hit back with an outstanding chance in the 63rd\xc2\xa0minute, when Johnson demolished a 35-yard free kick at the Honduran goal, but Valladares\xe2\x80\x99s fingertips were enough to push it off the post and deny the Portland Timbers captain the\xc2\xa0second goal of the night.</p>\n<ul>\n<li><strong><a href="http://matchcenter.mlssoccer.com/matchcenter/2015-11-13-canada-mens-national-team-vs-honduras/boxscore">BOXSCORE: GET PLAYER STATS FROM THE GAME</a></strong></li>\n</ul>\n<p>Another chance came 10 minutes later, when de Jong swung in a free kick that found Dejan Jakovic unmarked, but it took a late bounce and ended up going harmlessly wide. Honduras came right back down the field and had their\xc2\xa0own chance through substitute Mario Martinez, but his long-distance effort sailed high.</p>\n<p>Martinez came close again in the 76th\xc2\xa0minute, sending a long-range diagonal shot that nearly caught Borjan off his line, but the Canadian keeper got back to push it over the bar. Then, five minutes later, he launched another long-range effort that forced Borjan into a diving save.</p>\n<p>Despite Martinez\xe2\x80\x99s attempts to single-handedly get his team back in the game, Canada held on for a nervy final portion of the match to send the fans home happy. The outcome of Friday\xe2\x80\x99s game won\xe2\x80\x99t wash away years of bitter memories for Canada in World Cup qualifiers, but it certainly got their quest toward Russia 2018 off on the right foot.</p>\n</article><div class="gigya-comments" data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.8" id="article-comments"></div></img></div></div><div class="ad-wrapper" data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.1" id="matchcenter-recap-1"></div></div></div></section></div></section></main><div class="connection-warning" data-reactid=".240gvxnhhxc.a" style="pointer-events:none;">Connection Lost.
